# Community Builds (Overframe.gg, T3-equivalent, community-curated)
FORMAT: Each ## entry is one community-submitted build flagged `(community-curated, source: Overframe)`. Meta line: Role | Author | Votes | Forma | MR | Overframe build #ID. Role is one of `top` (highest community score for that item — meta/endgame pick), `utility` (title-matched support / CC / farming / stealth / subsume build), or `runner-up` (second highest score, alternative meta). For endgame queries (Steel Path, Netracells, Deep Archimedea, Eidolon, Profit-Taker, level-cap) prefer `top` or `runner-up`; quote `utility` only when the operator requests support / CC / farming / stealth / Helminth context. When enriched, ### Mod Loadout lists each slot as `- S<N> <Mod Name>` (mod names resolved from Overframe's mod catalog; rank, polarity, and drain are intentionally omitted — assume max rank unless the author guide says otherwise), followed by ### Author Guide containing the first ~800 chars of the author's build write-up. Treat as suggestions only — never override official stats from equipment/weapons/mods/export bundles. Bot output must still never list polarity or drain values.

# Overframe Community Builds — Warframes
Community-curated build snapshots scraped from Overframe.gg.
These are popular Tenno-submitted loadouts, NOT official game data.
Every entry is flagged `(community-curated, source: Overframe)` and must never override authoritative stats from equipment/weapons/mods/export bundles.
Each item carries up to three roles: `top` (highest score — meta/endgame pick), `utility` (title-matched support / CC / farming / stealth / subsume build), and `runner-up` (second highest score).
Prefer `top` or `runner-up` for endgame queries; use `utility` only when the request is for support / CC / farming / Helminth context.

### Author Guide
Can use fewer Forma if you have an Umbral Forma.
Here's the gist: [Ore Gaze] guarantees loot dropped at >=400% strength (with no upper limit). [Rubble Heap] lets you cast Landslide for free when you're at 1400 rubble collected. [Path of Statues] applies Petrify to enemies hit by Landslide.
We don't care too much about efficiency.
You'll be casting Landslide for free and the only other ability you'll be casting is Petrify.
But you'll be picking up Energy Orbs regularly enough to keep up the strength bonus from [Energy Conversion].
And use a status priming weapon to keep up the bonus from [Growing Power].
Duration definitely could use a bit of love so feel free to swap out [Arcane Energize] for [Molt Efficiency] if you want (the bonus to duration doesn't display correctly here).

## Day and Night Sleep/Nuke Switch Equinox \| Steel Path — Equinox Prime (community-curated, source: Overframe)
Role: top | Author: ninjase | Votes: 1090 | Forma: 2 | MR: 0 | Overframe build #212520

### Mod Loadout
- S1 Fleeting Expertise
- S2 Equilibrium
- S3 Stretch
- S4 Augur Reach
- S5 Primed Flow
- S6 Energy Transfer
- S7 Rolling Guard
- S8 Overextended
- S9 Corrosive Projection
- S10 Cunning Drift
- S11 Arcane Aegis
- S12 Molt Augmented

## INTRODUCTION This Steel Path build is focused around switching forms to take advantage of the survivability/crowd control of night form and Maim nuking of day form. Night mode allows you to crowd control entire maps by putting them to sleep with Rest, allowing you to kill them at your leisure to store damage as well as restore shields with Mend for shield gating. With the augment Energy Transfer, switching to day mode preserves the stored damage. Once you have stored sufficient damage and there is a good enemy density, switch to day form and deactivate 4 to nuke the map. ### Author Guide
How Nourish (2) works.
Casting Nourish (2) on different units gives you different buffs, they are as followed; - Heavy, flying or summoned units: Strike buff (Adds toxin damage to all attacks for nearby friendlies) - Melee units: Armor Buff (Deal toxin damage around friendlies whenever they take damage) - Ranged units: Energy Buff (Multiplies the energy gained for all nearby friendlies) The buff Nourish (2) you obtain is determined by which enemy was consumed first by feast, if multiple enemies were consumed by feast you can cycle through buffs by holding Nourish (2) down.
If you wish to have an additional 10% strength feel free to install a maxed Transient Fortitude (rank 10).
I chose a Rank 8 to have the buff as close to 1 minute duration possible.
You can easily hold 3 enemies

## Infinite Invis (0 Forma, No Primed Mods) — Loki (community-curated, source: Overframe)
Role: utility | Author: Touchstone | Votes: 38 | Forma: 0 | MR: 0 | Overframe build #30465

### Mod Loadout
- S1 (empty)
- S2 Vitality
- S3 Streamline
- S4 Continuity
- S5 Constitution
- S6 Augur Message
- S7 Fleeting Expertise
- S8 Narrow Minded
- S9 Energy Siphon
- S10 Thief's Wit

## The Case for Fleeting Expertise Maximizing Ability Efficiency at the expense of Ability Duration is more effective than not. With it on this build, Invisibility lasts for 26.52 seconds and costs 12.5 Energy per cast. While under the effects of Invisibility you will regenerate 15.912 Energy thanks to Energy Siphon, functionally allowing you to continue casting Invisibility for as long as you'd like. On the other hand, without it Invisibility lasts for 33.72 seconds and costs 35 Energy per cast. While under its effects you will regain 20.232 Energy. Unlike the build with it, this means that you run an Energy deficit every time you cast. So go forward with your infinite invisibility. Scan Kavats, I guess?

### Author Guide

Polarities: If the symbol on the mod is the same as the symbol in the slot, it doubles for aura or halves for regular mods. (Example Flow being half its normal cost, and Steel Charge being double) if a mod is of a different polarity it takes more capacity.
Aura: This Mod Slot is the only slot that is good to put a mod in regardless of the mod itself, It increases your capacity by the mods displayed amount in the top right corner.

Danse Macabre also has innate armor strip since it procs corrosive status on any armored enemies. By levelcap, enemies typically deal up to 1 million damage per shot, meaning each revolution of nine lasers deals 9 million damage after just one shot. If you absorb damage for a few seconds, you could absorb upwards of 10 to 50 million damage meaning each revolution deals 450 million damage total, enough to oneshot all enemies at levelcap without armor strip. # Overframe Community Builds — Archwings
Community-curated build snapshots scraped from Overframe.gg.
These are popular Tenno-submitted loadouts, NOT official game data.
Every entry is flagged `(community-curated, source: Overframe)` and must never override authoritative stats from equipment/weapons/mods/export bundles.
Each item carries up to three roles: `top` (highest score — meta/endgame pick), `utility` (title-matched support / CC / farming / stealth / subsume build), and `runner-up` (second highest score).
Prefer `top` or `runner-up` for endgame queries; use `utility` only when the request is for support / CC / farming / Helminth context.
Snapshot fetched 2026-05-15T19:58:48.835Z; up to 3 per item; enriched=yes.

## Railjack Amesha with Guide — Amesha (community-curated, source: Overframe)
Author: corgigoro | Votes: 115 | Forma: 3 | MR: 0 | Overframe build #12277

### Mod Loadout
- S1 Argon Plating
- S2 Efficient Transferral
- S3 Energy Amplifier
- S4 Auxiliary Power
- S5 Enhanced Durability
- S6 System Reroute
- S7 Hyperion Thrusters
- S8 Primed Morphic Transformer

### Author Guide
This is the standard build for Amesha for Railjack.
How to use Amesha: Activate 3 (Warding Grace), this will drain your energy but slow enemies and make you immune to status effects including getting knocked around.
Activate 4 (Vengeful Rush), this will restore energy when you take damage and is usually only used to get energy back when you are below 50%.
Activate 1, this will absorb any instance of damage, AOE or direct damage.
This skill keeps you alive.
Activate 2, this will create a shield to redirect all damage to the smaller bubble in the middle.
Damage taken by that bubble will heal anything inside it but you cannot shoot from out of it.
These two skills will allow you to survive everything other than one shots by missiles.
If your HP gets low, activate 2 (Benevolent Decoy).
...

Hello There, This need a little explanation...

Additional elemental damage is always welcome, as well as Status Chance, that's why I chosen those two.
We need to keep shooting so I added **Quick Reload **mod to reduce the pause between reloading.
Enjoy, THeMooN85

# Overframe Community Builds — Sentinels
Community-curated build snapshots scraped from Overframe.gg.
These are popular Tenno-submitted loadouts, NOT official game data.
Every entry is flagged `(community-curated, source: Overframe)` and must never override authoritative stats from equipment/weapons/mods/export bundles.
Each item carries up to three roles: `top` (highest score — meta/endgame pick), `utility` (title-matched support / CC / farming / stealth / subsume build), and `runner-up` (second highest score).
Prefer `top` or `runner-up` for endgame queries; use `utility` only when the request is for support / CC / farming / Helminth context.
Snapshot fetched 2026-05-15T19:58:48.835Z; up to 3 per item; enriched=yes.

## Max Survivability, Buff Smeeta — Smeeta Kavat (community-curated, source: Overframe)
Author: Arsonistic | Votes: 1235 | Forma: 6 | MR: 0 | Overframe build #8828

### Mod Loadout

- S4 Synth Fiber
- S5 Hastened Deflection
- S6 Link Vitality
- S7 Tek Assault
- S8 Tek Enhance
- S9 Primed Animal Instinct
- S10 Charm

### Author Guide
Hastened Deflection(+Shield Recharge) for better shield-gating invulnerability.
Shield-gating grants invulnerability when shield is broken.
The duration of invulnerability scales from 0.3 to 1 second depending on how much shield was left when it was broken.
Tek Enhance provides longer Charm buffs.
Synth Fiber adds some nice passive reload of weapons, and lets you pick up health orbs at max health, which has some synergies with Health Conversion and Equilibrium.
Check out my other builds on my profile.
Especially the "Generic" build series, which show the optimal builds for 90+% of weapons of that type.

## Steel Path Shredder - Status Squirting Energy Printer — Nautilus Prime (community-curated, source: Overframe)
Author: Beastlinator | Votes: 589 | Forma: 3 | MR: 0 | Overframe build #717223

### Mod Loadout
- S1 Primed Regen
- S2 Vacuum
- S3 Assault Mode
- S4 Cordon
- S5 Fired Up
- S6 Primed Animal Instinct
- S7 Manifold Bond
- S8 Momentous Bond
- S9 Contagious Bond
- S10 Duplex Bond

### Author Guide
Use My **Verglas Prime Build** for best results: **Groups, Kills, Prints Energy.** Credit to ninjase for making me aware how Manifold Bond works with mod order/ precept order.
The game reads your mods First Line, left to right and then second line left to right, therefore to ensure Manifold Bond reduces Cordon's cooldown, make sure to place Cordon above all other precepts. (previously I had Primed Regen above Cordon and I am unsure if that has an effect, but I am certain having Cordon be first in precept order works with Manifold Bond.
I believe Primed Regen/Regen and Vacuum are Passive Precepts so the cooldown from Manifold Bond *should* ignore them, but to be safe I moved Cordon to first priority) Primed Regen - We don't have room for defenses. good
...

Hello there, With Abyss of [Dagath] Update came much needed changes with our companions.
Because of that, we can also change their weapons, so they can actually become useful and... deadly.
So why galv. mods?
Good question... companions can't stack them, BUT(T)! we can.
We can stack those bonuses for them.
How does this work?
You can stack galv. mods bonuses if your weapon matches your companion weapon.
WAIT, WHAT?
OK, listen to me... if you are using a rifle weapon, your companion also needs to use a rifle.
If you change your weapon for shotgun, you should also change your companion weapon for shotgun.
GET IT?!
I hope so.
Enjoy!

- S8 Radiated Reload

### Author Guide
Hello there, With Abyss of Dagath Update came much needed changes with our companions.
Because of that, we can also change their weapons, so they can actually become useful and... deadly.
So why galv. mods?
Good question... companions can't stack them, BUT(T)! we can.
We can stack those bonuses for them.
How does this work?
You can stack galv. mods bonuses if your weapon matches your companion weapon.
WAIT, WHAT?
OK, listen to me... if you are using a rifle weapon, your companion also needs to use a rifle.
If you change your weapon for shotgun, you should also change your companion weapon for shotgun.
GET IT?!
I hope so.
Enjoy!
THeMooN85

Because of that, we can also change their weapons, so they can actually become useful and... deadly.
So why galv. mods?
Good question... companions can't stack them, BUT(T)! we can.
We can stack those bonuses for them.
How does this work?
You can stack galv. mods bonuses if your weapon matches your companion weapon.
WAIT, WHAT?
OK, listen to me... if you are using a rifle weapon, your companion also needs to use a rifle.
If you change your weapon for shotgun, you should also change your companion weapon for shotgun.
GET IT?!
I hope so.
Enjoy!
THeMooN85

Only minor benefits from having a maxed out rank. - Hunter Recovery: The healing this offers to your warframe makes it completive with Fetch.
Hard to pick. - Hunter Synergy: The critical chance from this mod is based on your primary weapon (regardless of it being drawn or holstered) and added last.
